            <v:rating>
              <v:severity>High</v:severity>
            </v:rating>
            <v:rating>
              <v:score>
                <v:base>6.5</v:base>

                <v:exploitability>8</v:exploitability>

            </v:rating>

                <v:impact>5.9</v:impact>
                <v:exploitability>2.8</v:exploitability>
              </v:score>
              <v:method>CVSSv3</v:method>

            </v:rating>
          </v:ratings>
